< Text>
I have had a number of vets and emergency vets over the years and Dr. Yang and his staff have consistently provided solid service.

At Thornhill Pet Hospital you don't get pushed into buying extra procedures or special foods and supplements. He reminds me of the country vet that I went to when I lived in Northern CA. They Let you know when something is outside of their scope (specialty surgery) but they are they general practitioners that can make the difference in the quality of life of your loved pets.

Dr. Yang has helped lots of folks that rescue animals. Pre-COVID I would see them in the lobby with the animals. I am no different.  I rescued one dog that needed aggressive skin cancer tumors removed and was underweight and ill from lack of food and horrible fleas. Dr, Yang removed several of the worst of the tumors getting clear margins and predicted that the dog would live just six months. 18 months later she needed more tumors removed and he said that it had to be her last surgery as she was old, frail and now how some scar tissue making surgery more difficult. Well, she is alive another 18 months later and frailer but happy and enjoying life.

Go ahead and get an appointment with this vet for your pet and know that you are doing right by them.</Text>

<Rate>5</Rate>< text>
Best vet practice I've ever been to.  Dr. Yang is very thorough, calm and takes the time to explain things well.  He has even called me after office hours in response to questions.  The rest of the staff (go Alicia and Vicky!) are great, super nice and helpful.  They will even file your pet insurance claims for you which is really nice.  The prices here are good, I would say below average for the Bay Area.  They try to give you discounts on care/meds whenever possible also.  I would pay more and be no less happy, especially when you consider the state of veterinary care today - very overworked and underpaid.  Pet health care costs have been rising along with human health costs due to many similar reasons: new technology, high cost of drugs and high education costs/debt loads for providers among other reasons, but vets make significantly less money than human physicians.  The level of service provided by Thornhill is even more impressive when you take that into account with their good prices.

And I'll also put in a plug for pet insurance:  If for no other reason than if, like me, you don't ever want to be put in a position where you have to take money into account when deciding on your pet's medical care<//text>

Usually I would be the first to slam Domino's and everything they stand for, however things have changed with this place. The food has improved quite a bit this past year and the menu has expanded in a good way. While the beverage selection remains poor their pizza has become quite good. Domino's always had good delivery service, but now they have good pizza as well. I used to feel sick, bloated, and toxic after consuming anything made by Domino's. The quality of the ingredients was bad. They have changed that and it now seems like actual food fit for humans. This is not a high end pizza or an Italian cuisine restaurant by an means, but if you want a decent pizza delivered for a fair price you can now trust them to come through. 7 out of 10</review>

<pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNwqGdVMCPooXX4RgVbtuUQ0DWNCXstDvwnReFS=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMtGOM3SYm3n1AULDlHI-khwGAgMyPikmqrg5OJ=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNo2m_1oIbmciLBOZgpawyiM6gzq3j_-gwYnGNW=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pictures><date>1558714763350< /date><review>Rikas is a small restaurant serving delicious peruvian fare, so don't come here with a large group. Because of its size, it seems like most people come here for pickup.

Food:
*PRO TIP: Douse everything in the Aji verde sauce. That thing will make ANYTHING DELICIOUS*
1) Ceviche Mixto - I haven't had bad peruvian ceviche yet. It's one of those peruvian staples that's a safe solid option wherever you go for Peruvian.
2) Lomo saltado - it wasn't perfect, but delicious. The beef could've been more tender, but the flavor was on point. The fries were pretty substantial and filling.
3) Chicharron - I was expecting crispy skin similar to chips, but it was actually small pieces of juicy, battered, fried chicken. The batter wasn't too heavy either. Excellent! The sauces were excellent too.

Service: Pretty slow. One of my friends got his order of lomo saltado and the three of us got ours like 20-30 minutes later, but they did apologize and offer us some soda.

Parking: You can barely call that a parking lot in front. Street parking is a challenge. Seems like people take one of those scooters or use one of the delivery services to get the food from here because the parking situation is less than ideal.

Note to self: Wanted to try the pollo a la brasa but they were out, so I will be back to try it<//review>< username>

<name>Steve Cha</name><date>1603662232658</date><Rating>5</Rating><review>Rikas Peruvian restaurant is like the 5th or 6th Peruvian restaurant I've been to in LA. It's interesting because it's located in Koreatown. But this little Peruvian restaurant packs a bunch. I enjoyed it a lot. It's like classic Peruvian comfort food. If you guys haven't tried their ceviche mixto, it is a must try. It's probably the best Peruvian ceviche I'd had in LA. Nice fresh raw fish, and the sourness to the juice was just about right. Their chaufa pollo, or chicken fried rice, was also another knockout. It's safe to say that this is the best fried rice I've had outside of any Asian restaurant. Haha. Their lomo saltado was also pretty solid. Great sauce, fries, and steak.

In all, I would highly recommend Rikas if you are in town. It is one of the best Peruvian restaurants in the area. You'll feel so great after eating the food here. The chef Jose is also a hospitable man. Look out for him if you come here. I shot a Youtube video of my experience at Rikas, which you can find on my Youtube channel Rockstar Eater.</review>< Pics>

< name>
Linh Do<//name>
<time>1529541587430</time><Rate>2< /Rate><review>You know they give out free milk tea if you write a review right? That means you can't really trust the review system anymore! Well, I got fooled by all the advertisement. Advice to people who want to try good Vietnamese food: this is not the place!!!

Rear parking is limited, side parking is scary and weird.
Inside decor is nice.

Service is bad! They forgot about half of our order, then the waitress came out and ask us "oh the food is not out yet?" Uhmmm I don't work here girl, idk?!!!

Food:
Bun cha Hanoi is supposed to be the signature dish of any Hanoi restaurant here in OC, but they made it poorly: the meat cake was dry, the fish sauce was really salty... If you know Vietnamese cuisine you know that the sauce is the most important part of many many dishes. They failed with this signature one.
Bun dau mam tom was a 3.5/5, I have to give it to them on the mam tom though, they made a good job with the sauce on this dish. Just the cha com was terrible, it's like eating a very moist sticky rice cake being fried...
Bun ca was a disappointment! The soup isn't sour enough. It seems to me like they don't put in the effort of making the different broth for different noodle soup. Bun ca has its own kind of broth, pho has its own kind of broth, bun rieu has its own kind of broth....

In conclusion, I don't like it!!! You might get better dishes than we did maybe.... At your own risk you come in!< /review>< Pics>

<user_id>115272165125261998433< /user_id>< Name>
Kimmie Nguyen< /Name>
<Time>1526069562779< /Time><rate>5<//rate><review>I really enjoy dining here at any time of the day.
It is absolutely delicious and the presentation of the food is well represented.

I was craving Bun Cha Ha Noi and found this restaraunt on yelp. I wanted to try a new restaraunt and drove here. The restaraunt is "not in your face" and from the direction I was heading, I had to make a U turn. I did not have trouble finding parking, but this place could get packed.

We were quicklyy seated and the staff were very nice and polite. We sat at the booth and it was spacious. They hire just the right amount of staff that you do not need to chase them down if you needed something. The menu was straightforward and there were photos to go along with the food items. I ordered Bun Cha Ha Noi and my mom ordered a variety platter. The food came out very quickly. The food presentation was adorable with the banana leaf and so. They put a whole bottle of water on your table for your and their convenience. The cups are cute and perfect size.

Bun Cha Ha Noi had the right amount of additives to it, it was very flavorful with vermicelli noodles and the meat were fantastic. They make it just right and perfected the dish that their was no pork smell to it. I really enjoyed it and so did my mom. I have not tried their desserts but can guarantee that their main dishes are worth the drive, at least for me since I am not around the area. I also signed up for their phone list to earn credits to receive freebies, it is a neat concept that I do not see most Vietnamese restaraunt does.

We had such a great meal, my mom asked me to drive her back here again the next time. And again, we had a good time, it was not packed when we arrived in the morning. The service, again, was excellent and the food was yummy. I highly reccommend this restaraunt.</review>< pictures>
